julia bacha: when i first heard about the story of budrus , i was surprised that the international media had failed to cover the extraordinary set of events that happened seven years ago , in 2003 .	朱利亞•巴克:當我第一次聽到關於布德魯的故事時 , 我很驚訝 , 在2003年 , 國際媒體已經失敗了 。
what was even more surprising was the fact that budrus was successful .	更令人驚訝的是 , 布德魯斯成功了 。
the residents , after 10 months of peaceful resistance , convinced the israeli government to move the route of the barrier off their lands and to the green line , which is the internationally recognized boundary between israel and the palestinian territories .	數十個月後 , 阿拉伯人和巴勒斯坦的國際同理協會 , 把土地和巴勒斯坦的國際分解在土地上 , 和巴勒斯坦的軍隊合作 。
the resistance in budrus has since spread to villages across the west bank and to palestinian neighborhoods in jerusalem .	巴勒斯坦的鄰居在耶路撒冷 , 巴勒斯坦鄰居在耶路撒冷 。
yet the media remains mostly silent on these stories .	但媒體仍然在這些故事中最沉默 。
this silence carries profound consequences for the likelihood that nonviolence can grow , or even survive , in palestine .	這種沉默的後果會造成很嚴重的後果 , 不暴力可能會成長 , 或甚至存活在巴勒斯坦 。
violent resistance and nonviolent resistance share one very important thing in common ; they are both a form of theater seeking an audience to their cause .	暴力抗拒和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性 ,
if violent actors are the only ones constantly getting frontpage covers and attracting international attention to the palestinian issue , it becomes very hard for nonviolent leaders to make the case to their communities that civil disobedience is a viable option in addressing their plight .	假如暴力的領導者 , 會讓這個案件變得非常困難 , 因為非暴力的領導者 , 會讓這個案件變得非常困難 , 因為非暴力的領導者 , 會讓他們對非暴力的領導者做出這個案例 , 讓他們對非暴力的領導者做出這個案例 , 讓它們的社區變得非常困難 , 因為非暴力的領導者 , 會讓他們對非暴力的領導者做出這個案例 , 讓它們的社區變得非常困難 。
the power of attention is probably going to come as no surprise to the parents in the room .	注意力的注意力可能在房間裡沒有驚訝 。
the surest way to make your child throw increasingly louder tantrums is by giving him attention the first time he throws a fit .	若要讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 就會讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈 。
the tantrum will become what childhood psychologists call a functional behavior , since the child has learned that he can get parental attention out of it .	腫瘤會變成兒童心理學家稱之為功能性行為 , 因為孩子們知道他能得到父母注意 。
parents can incentivize or disincentivize behavior simply by giving or withdrawing attention to their children .	父母可以預期或把注意力放在他們的孩子身上 。
but that's true for adults too .	但對成年人來說也是如此 。
in fact , the behavior of entire communities and countries can be influenced , depending on where the international community chooses to focus its attention .	事實上 , 整個社區的行為和國家都能受到影響 , 包括整個社區和國家的行為 , 都影響到國際社群的行為 。
i believe that at the core of ending the conflict in the middle east and bringing peace is for us to transform nonviolence into a functional behavior by giving a lot more attention to the nonviolent leaders on the ground today .	我相信 , 在中東和平的關鍵行為 , 將非暴力的領導者帶給我們 , 將非暴力的領導者帶給我們 。
in the course of taking my film to villages in the west bank , in gaza and in east jerusalem , i have seen the impact that even one documentary film can have in influencing the transformation .	在加薩和東耶魯撒冷 , 我看到了這場景象的影響 , 包括在加薩和東耶路撒冷的影像 , 我也看到了影響到這個轉變的影響 。
in a village called wallajeh , which sits very close to jerusalem , the community was facing a very similar plight to budrus .	在一個村落裡 , 一個叫做牆拉jeh的社區 , 非常接近jeh , 這個村莊很像布德魯斯 。
they were going to be surrounded , lose a lot of their lands and not have freedom of access , either to the west bank or jerusalem .	他們會被周圍圍繞 , 失去了許多土地 , 沒有自由 , 也沒有自由 , 也沒有自由 , 也沒有自由 , 也沒有自由 , 也沒有自由 。
they had been using nonviolence for about two years but had grown disenchanted since nobody was paying attention .	他們用非暴力的兩年來 , 因為沒有人會注意 。
so we organized a screening .	所以我們組織了螢幕 。
a week later , they held the most wellattended and disciplined demonstration to date .	一週後 , 他們重建了最好的特徵 , 和他們對約會最好的解答 。
the organizers say that the villagers , upon seeing the story of budrus documented in a film , felt that there were indeed people following what they were doing , that people cared .	組織者說 , 村民們在電影裡看到了關於布德魯斯的故事 , 在電影中 , 人們會看到他們在電影裡所做的 , 發現他們正在做的事 , 人們會追隨他們所做的事 , 感覺到他們正在做的事 , 人們會追隨他們所做的 。
so they kept on going .	所以他們繼續下去 。
on the israeli side , there is a new peace movement called solidariot , which means solidarity in hebrew .	在右邊 , 有一個新的和平運動叫做 「 蘇格蘭人 」 , 意思是 「 伊斯蘭 」 。
the leaders of this movement have been using budrus as one of their primary recruiting tools .	這種運動的領導者正在使用布德魯斯 , 用布德魯斯的領導者 , 使用布德魯斯的領導者 。
they report that israelis who had never been active before , upon seeing the film , understand the power of nonviolence and start joining their activities .	他們報導了非暴力的權利 , 開始加入他們的活動 。
the examples of wallajeh and the solidariot movement show that even a smallbudget independent film can play a role in transforming nonviolence into a functional behavior .	和伊斯蘭運動的例子 , 甚至是一小預算一支獨立電影可以扮演一個角色 , 改變非暴力行為的例子 。
now imagine the power that big media players could have if they started covering the weekly nonviolent demonstrations happening in villages like bil'in , ni'lin , wallajeh , in jerusalem neighborhoods like sheikh jarrah and silwan the nonviolent leaders would become more visible , valued and effective in their work .	現在 , 想像一下 , 大媒體玩家的力量會變得更有價值 , 和他們的工作中有所不同 , 不暴力的領導者會變得更有價值、價值和有效率 。
i believe that the most important thing is to understand that if we don't pay attention to these efforts , they are invisible , and it's as if they never happened .	我相信最重要的事情是要了解如果我們不把注意力投入這些努力 , 他們就會被隱形 , 不管他們從未發生過 。
but i have seen first hand that if we do , they will multiply .	但是我看到第一隻手 , 如果我們這麼做 , 它們會多樣化 。
if they multiply , their influence will grow in the overall israelipalestinian conflict .	如果他們多大 , 他們的影響會成長在巴勒斯坦衝突中 。
and theirs is the kind of influence that can finally unblock the situation .	他們的影響力可以終於阻止這個情況 。
these leaders have proven that nonviolence works in places like budrus .	這些領導者已經證明非暴力工作就像布德魯一樣 。
let's give them attention so they can prove it works everywhere .	讓我們給他們注意力 , 讓它們能證明它的工作 。
simon sinek has a simple but powerful model for inspirational leadership all starting with a golden circle and the question " why ? " his examples include apple , martin luther king , and the wright brothers . . .	西蒙斯坦克有個簡單的例子 , 包括蘋果、馬丁•路德•金恩 , 和 「 為什麼 ? 」 他的例子包括蘋果、馬丁路德•金恩 , 和 「 為什麼 ? 」 他的例子包括蘋果、馬丁路德•金恩 , 和 「 為什麼 ? 」
bullseye , business , entrepreneur , leadership , sales , selling , success	商業、企業、商業、企業家、領導力、財富、企業、商業、企業家、領導力、財富、商業、企業家、領導力、財富、企業、商業、企業家、領導力、財富、
simon sinek: how great leaders inspire action	西蒙斯坦克:偉大的領導者鼓勵行動 。
how do you explain when things don't go as we assume ?	你要如何解釋當事情不如我們假設時會怎麼解釋 ?
or better , how do you explain when others are able to achieve things that seem to defy all of the assumptions ?	或更好 , 你怎麼解釋 , 當其他人能夠達成這些假設時 , 會怎麼解釋 ?
for example: why is apple so innovative ?	例如:為什麼蘋果這麼創新 ?
year after year , after year , after year , they're more innovative than all their competition .	一年 , 一年後 , 一年後 , 他們比所有競爭的競爭都更創新 。
and yet , they're just a computer company .	然而 , 他們只是電腦公司 。
they're just like everyone else .	他們就像其他人一樣 。
they have the same access to the same talent , the same agencies , the same consultants , the same media .	他們有相同的能力 , 同一群體 , 同一群 , 同一間公司 , 同一間媒體 。
then why is it that they seem to have something different ?	為什麼他們似乎有不同 ?
why is it that martin luther king led the civil rights movement ?	為什麼是馬丁路德•金恩德王國王領民權利運動 ?
he wasn't the only man who suffered in a precivil rights america , and he certainly wasn't the only great orator of the day .	他不是唯一的美國人 , 他肯定不是唯一的美國人 , 他肯定不是唯一的美國人 , 他肯定不是唯一的男人 。
and why is it that the wright brothers were able to figure out controlled , powered man flight when there were certainly other teams who were better qualified , better funded . . .	為何 , 權力飛行器也能找出控制權力的人 , 更好的資金 , 更好的資金 , 更好資金 。
and they didn't achieve powered man flight , and the wright brothers beat them to it .	他們沒有人飛行 , 妻子兄弟們打敗他們 。
there's something else at play here .	這裡還有其他東西 。
about three and a half years ago i made a discovery .	大約三年半前 , 我做了一個發現 。
and this discovery profoundly changed my view on how i thought the world worked , and it even profoundly changed the way in which i operate in it .	這個發現深深地改變了我的觀點 , 甚至徹底改變了我的觀點 , 甚至徹底改變了我的觀點 。
as it turns out , there's a pattern .	結果發現 , 有一種模式 。
as it turns out , all the great and inspiring leaders and organizations in the world whether it's apple or martin luther king or the wright brothers they all think , act and communicate the exact same way .	結果發現 , 所有偉大、激勵領袖和組織在世界各地的領導者和組織 , 不論是蘋果或馬丁路德金或馬丁路德•金或馬丁路德•金或馬丁路德•金或馬丁路德•金或馬丁路德•金或馬丁•路德•金或馬丁•路德•金或馬丁•路德•金或馬丁•路德•金恩 ,
and it's the complete opposite to everyone else .	這完全相反對其他人 。
all i did was codify it , and it's probably the world's simplest idea .	我所做的是 , 它可能是世界上最簡單的概念 。
i call it the golden circle .	我稱它為黃金圈 。
why ? how ? what ?	為什麼 ? 怎麼樣 ?
this little idea explains why some organizations and some leaders are able to inspire where others aren't .	這個小點子解釋了為什麼有些組織和一些組織有一些組織 , 有些組織和一些領導者能夠鼓舞其他人 。
let me define the terms really quickly .	讓我定義這個詞很快 。
every single person , every single organization on the planet knows what they do , 100 percent .	每個人 , 每一個組織都知道他們所做的事 , 百分之百 。
some know how they do it , whether you call it your differentiated value proposition or your proprietary process or your usp .	有些人知道他們如何做 , 不論你是否稱它為 「 不論你 」 、 「 不論 」 、 「 不論 」 、 「 不論 」 、 「 不論 」 、 「 不論 」 、
but very , very few people or organizations know why they do what they do .	但 , 非常少人或組織知道為什麼他們會這麼做 。
and by " why " i don't mean " to make a profit . "	為 「 為何 」 , 我並不表示 「 為何 」 的意思是 「 為何 」 。
that's a result . it's always a result .	這是結果 , 結果是結果 。
by " why , " i mean: what's your purpose ?	順道一提: 「 為什麼 ? 」 意思是:你的目的是什麼 ?
what's your cause ? what's your belief ?	你的信念是什麼 ? 你的信念是什麼 ?
why does your organization exist ?	為什麼你的組織存在 ?
why do you get out of bed in the morning ?	為什麼你早上早上起床 ?
and why should anyone care ?	為什麼有人關心 ?
well , as a result , the way we think , the way we act , the way we communicate is from the outside in .	結果是 , 我們所做的 , 就是從外面來到外面 。
it's obvious . we go from the clearest thing to the fuzziest thing .	很明顯的 , 我們從最明顯的角度來看 , 很明顯 。
but the inspired leaders and the inspired organizations regardless of their size , regardless of their industry all think , act and communicate from the inside out .	但鼓舞的領導者和靈感組織 , 不管他們在哪裡 , 不論他們的產業 , 不管是誰 , 不管他們在哪裡 , 不論他們的產業 。
let me give you an example .	讓我舉個例子 。
i use apple because they're easy to understand and everybody gets it .	我使用蘋果 , 因為他們很容易理解 , 每個人都得到它 。
if apple were like everyone else , a marketing message from them might sound like this: " we make great computers .	如果蘋果跟其他人一樣 , 市場的訊息來自他們聽起來像這樣: 「 我們製造了很棒的電腦 。
they're beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	它們很美麗設計 , 簡單使用和使用者友善 。
want to buy one ? " " meh . "	想買一個嗎 ? 「 啊 ! 」
and that's how most of us communicate .	那就是我們大部分人溝通的方式 。
that's how most marketing is done , that's how most sales is done and that's how most of us communicate interpersonally .	這是最多的銷售量 , 最多的銷售量是最多的 , 那就是我們最多的銷售量 。
we say what we do , we say how we're different or how we're better and we expect some sort of a behavior , a purchase , a vote , something like that .	我們說我們是怎麼做的 , 我們會說我們是怎麼樣的 , 我們會說我們是怎麼樣的 , 我們會說我們是怎樣的 , 或更好的 , 我們會說我們是怎樣的 , 或我們如何做比較好的 , 我們會說我們是怎樣的 , 或我們如何做 , 或更好的 ,
here's our new law firm: we have the best lawyers with the biggest clients , we always perform for our clients who do business with us .	這是我們的新法律:我們有最好的律師 , 最好的律師 , 我們總是對我們的客戶做事業 。
here's our new car: it gets great gas mileage , it has leather seats , buy our car .	這是我們的新車:它有很棒的電梯 , 買我們的車子 。
here's how apple actually communicates .	這是蘋果如何溝通 。
" everything we do , we believe in challenging the status quo .	「 我們所做的一切 , 我們相信挑戰地位 。
we believe in thinking differently .	我們相信在思考不同 。
the way we challenge the status quo is by making our products beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	我們挑戰的是 , 用和使用者友善的方式來設計 , 簡單使用使用和使用者 。
we just happen to make great computers .	我們只是為了製造好的電腦 。
want to buy one ? "	想買一個嗎 ? 」
totally different right ? you're ready to buy a computer from me .	完全不同 ? 你準備好要買一台電腦 。
all i did was reverse the order of the information .	我所做的就是把這些資訊傳遞給資訊 。
what it proves to us is that people don't buy what you do ; people buy why you do it .	這證明了我們是人們不買你做的事 , 人們不買你做的事 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做的事 , 他們買了你做的事 。
this explains why every single person in this room is perfectly comfortable buying a computer from apple .	這解釋為什麼每個人在這個房間裡的每個人都非常舒適地買電腦 。
but we're also perfectly comfortable buying an mp3 player from apple , or a phone from apple , or a dvr from apple .	但是我們也非常舒適 , 用蘋果的手機 , 或是來自蘋果的手機 , 或來自蘋果的手機 , 或來自蘋果的手機 , 或來自蘋果的手機 。
but , as i said before , apple's just a computer company .	但 , 如我之前所說的 , 蘋果只是電腦公司 。
there's nothing that distinguishes them structurally from any of their competitors .	沒有任何人都可以從他們的競爭者身上學到什麼 。
their competitors are all equally qualified to make all of these products .	他們的競爭者都等於製造這些產品 。
in fact , they tried .	事實上 , 他們嘗試了 。
a few years ago , gateway came out with flat screen tvs .	幾年前 , 格雷特•雷特在電視上發表了 。
they're eminently qualified to make flat screen tvs .	他們很高興能發出螢幕電視 。
they've been making flat screen monitors for years .	幾年來 , 他們都在製作廣告螢幕 。

it's what they believed about america that got them to travel in a bus for eight hours to stand in the sun in washington in the middle of august .	他們相信美國 , 讓他們在華盛頓在華盛頓的八小時內 , 到處在華盛頓的中間 。
it's what they believed , and it wasn't about black versus white: 25 percent of the audience was white .	這是他們相信的 , 而不是黑人的白人:25%的觀眾是白人 。
dr . king believed that there are two types of laws in this world: those that are made by a higher authority and those that are made by man .	金恩相信有兩種法律:這些是由一個較高的法律 , 由於人民的法律 。
and not until all the laws that are made by man are consistent with the laws that are made by the higher authority will we live in a just world .	直到所有法律都是由男性的法律所組成的法律所組成的法律 , 由於我們所擁有的法律 , 由男性和法律所組成的法律 , 以致於我們所擁有的法律 。
it just so happened that the civil rights movement was the perfect thing to help him bring his cause to life .	就這樣 , 民權運動是完美的 , 才能幫助他帶來生命 。
we followed , not for him , but for ourselves .	我們追蹤了 , 不是為了他 , 而是為了我們自己 。
and , by the way , he gave the " i have a dream " speech , not the " i have a plan " speech .	順便一提 , 他給了我一個夢想 , 不是 「 我有一個夢想 」 , 不是 「 我有一個夢想 」 。

because there are leaders and there are those who lead .	因為有領導人 , 也有領導者 。
leaders hold a position of power or authority , but those who lead inspire us .	領導人會鼓勵我們 , 但那些領導人鼓勵我們 。
whether they're individuals or organizations , we follow those who lead , not because we have to , but because we want to .	不論他們是個人或組織 , 我們會追蹤那些領導的人 , 而不是因為我們要去 。
we follow those who lead , not for them , but for ourselves .	我們追蹤那些領導的人 , 不是為了他們 , 而是為了自己 。
and it's those who start with " why " that have the ability to inspire those around them or find others who inspire them .	那些來自 「 為什麼 」 的能力 , 能夠啟發他們 , 或找到其他靈感的人 。

brain , cognitive science , exploration , neuroscience , science	大腦、科學、探索、神經科學、探索、神經科學 。

when we park in a big parking lot , how do we remember where we parked our car ?	當我們公園開車時 , 我們如何記得我們停車在哪裡 ?

and we're going to try to understand what's happening in his brain .	我們要試著了解他腦內發生的事 。
so we'll start with the hippocampus , shown in yellow , which is the organ of memory .	我們從海馬迴開始 , 看看黃色 , 這是記憶的器官 。
if you have damage there , like in alzheimer's , you can't remember things including where you parked your car .	如果你有損傷 , 像是阿茲海默症 , 你無法記得一些東西包括你停車的地方 。

and like the rest of the brain , it's made of neurons .	就像其他大腦的神經元一樣 。
so the human brain has about a hundred billion neurons in it .	人類大腦有大約一百億個神經元 。
and the neurons communicate with each other by sending little pulses or spikes of electricity via connections to each other .	神經元會互相互相溝通 , 與彼此相互溝通 。
the hippocampus is formed of two sheets of cells , which are very densely interconnected .	海馬體是由兩個細胞組成的 , 它們是非常密切的 。
and scientists have begun to understand how spatial memory works by recording from individual neurons in rats or mice while they forage or explore an environment looking for food .	科學家已經開始了解 , 透過記錄從個人神經元的神經元中 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 或老鼠 , 才能了解大腦如何運作 。
so we're going to imagine we're recording from a single neuron in the hippocampus of this rat here .	所以 , 我們要想像我們正在記錄從一個神經元的神經元 , 到這裡的一個神經元 。
and when it fires a little spike of electricity , there's going to be a red dot and a click .	當它發出電力時 , 會有一個紅點和點子 。
so what we see is that this neuron knows whenever the rat has gone into one particular place in its environment .	所以 , 我們看到的是 , 神經元知道 , 當這個神經元知道 , 當雷射進入一個特定的地方時 , 這種神經元知道 。
and it signals to the rest of the brain by sending a little electrical spike .	它訊號到大腦的訊號 , 傳送一個小電管 。
so we could show the firing rate of that neuron as a function of the animal's location .	所以我們可以展示出神經元的功能 , 以神經元為基礎 。
and if we record from lots of different neurons , we'll see that different neurons fire when the animal goes in different parts of its environment , like in this square box shown here .	如果我們從不同神經元的角度來看 , 我們會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 , 我們會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 , 會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 , 我們會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 , 會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 , 我們會看到不同神經元的不同神經元 。
so together they form a map for the rest of the brain , telling the brain continually , " where am i now within my environment ? "	所以 , 他們在我的環境中建立了一幅地圖 , 告訴大腦: 「 我現在在哪裡 ? 」

the one below likes to fire whenever there's a wall close by to the south .	一旦有一座牆接近南方 , 就會有一座牆 。
and if you put another wall inside the box , then the cell fires in both place wherever there's a wall to the south as the animal explores around in its box .	如果你把另一個牆壁放在盒子裡 , 在那裡 , 細胞就在盒子裡圍繞著它的牆壁 。

and what you see , for example , if the flag was where that cross was in a small square environment , and then if you ask people where it was , but you've made the environment bigger , where they think the flag had been stretches out in exactly the same way that the place cell firing stretched out .	舉例來說 , 如果旗幟在一個小型的平方環境上 , 你看到的是 , 如果旗幟在一個小平方環境上 , 會發現 , 如果旗幟在一個小平方環境上 , 就會發現 , 如果旗幟在一個小平方環境上 , 就會發現 , 當旗幟在一個小平方環境上 , 就會出現在一個小平方環境上 。
it's as if you remember where the flag was by storing the pattern of firing across all of your place cells at that location , and then you can get back to that location by moving around so that you best match the current pattern of firing of your place cells with that stored pattern .	正如你所想的 , 當你記得在那個地方的軌道上 , 你就可以回到那個地點 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 , 然後你就可以回到那個地點 , 然後你就可以回到那個地點 , 然後你就可以回到那個地方的軌道 。

and if you record from several grid cells shown here in different colors each one has a gridlike firing pattern across the environment , and each cell's gridlike firing pattern is shifted slightly relative to the other cells .	如果你從幾種不同的顏色開始 , 每個細胞的神經細胞都在不同顏色中 , 每個細胞的特徵 , 都在不同顏色中 , 每個細胞的神經細胞都在不同顏色中 , 每個細胞的網絡都在不同顏色 , 每個細胞都在不同顏色 。
so the red one fires on this grid and the green one on this one and the blue on on this one .	所以紅色的紅色是這張圖上的紅色 , 上面的紅色則是這張圖上的紅色 。
so together , it's as if the rat can put a virtual grid of firing locations across its environment a bit like the latitude and longitude lines that you'd find on a map , but using triangles .	所以 , 相同的 , 像拉丁和長期的線條 , 你在地圖上找到的圖像 , 但使用三角形 。
and as it moves around , the electrical activity can pass from one of these cells to the next cell to keep track of where it is , so that it can use its own movements to know where it is in its environment .	隨著它移動 , 電活動可以從一個細胞到下一個細胞 , 到下一個細胞 , 讓它可以通過這些細胞去追蹤它 , 所以它可以通過這些細胞去追蹤它 , 這樣它就可以通過這些細胞來追蹤它 。
do people have grid cells ?	人們有網幹細胞嗎 ?
well because all of the gridlike firing patterns have the same axes of symmetry , the same orientations of grid , shown in orange here , it means that the net activity of all of the grid cells in a particular part of the brain should change according to whether we're running along these six directions or running along one of the six directions in between .	由於這些神經元素的特定部分是腦部內部的特定部分 , 意味著神經活動 , 包括對稱的神經元素 , 它意味著 , 神經細胞的特定部分是大腦內部的特定部分 , 意味著神經活動 , 每一部分的神經活動 , 都應該改變我們在哪個方向 , 或跑到六個方向 。

he's probably remembering where his car was in terms of the distances and directions to extended buildings and boundaries around the location where he parked .	他可能記得他的車子在哪裡 , 遠離地點和方向 , 讓建築物和邊界的距離 , 讓他停下來 。

so it may be that the neural mechanisms for representing the space around us are also used for generating visual imagery so that we can recreate the spatial scene , at least , of the events that have happened to us when we want to imagine them .	所以 , 可能是神經機制 , 讓我們想要想像它們時 , 可能是神經機制 。
so if this was happening , your memories could start by place cells activating each other via these dense interconnections and then reactivating boundary cells to create the spatial structure of the scene around your viewpoint .	所以 , 如果發生了 , 你的記憶可以從各個細胞開始 , 讓細胞產生在你周圍的環境內部的結構 。

another kind of cell , head direction cells , which i didn't mention yet , they fire like a compass according to which way you're facing .	另一種類型的細胞 , 我沒有提到 , 它們會像同事一樣 , 會讓你面對的方向 。

so this is just one example of a new era really in cognitive neuroscience where we're beginning to understand psychological processes like how you remember or imagine or even think in terms of the actions of the billions of individual neurons that make up our brains .	這只是一個例子 , 一個新的時代 , 我們開始了解心理過程 , 像是你記得或想像或想像 , 甚至認為在數十億個神經元中 , 我們開始了解心理過程 。

imagine a global security driven by collaboration among agencies , government , the private sector and the public . that's not just the distant hope of opensource fans , it's the vision of james stavridis , the supreme commander of nato , who shares vivid moments from recent military history to explain why security of the future should be built with bridges rather than walls .	想像一個全球安全 , 來自最近的軍事歷史來解釋為何安全的未來應該要建造橋樑 , 而非牆壁 , 而非牆壁 。
collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作、全球議題、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭 , 和平、政治、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭 。
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆斯•史維里德:娜托斯•史維里斯•史維里德:娜多是如何最普遍的國際安全局 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我要講一點關於開放資源安全 , 因為我們必須在這個21世紀更好的安全 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我開始說 , 咱們來回二十世紀 , 看看二十世紀 , 看看二十世紀 , 感覺如何對我們有安全的影響 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是平衡的北方 , 北方是北方的北方 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	在1916年 , 在1916年 , 超過3000000000000000000人被殺死 , 大約有七十萬人死亡 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你在第二次世界大戰結束後 , 你看到了兩百萬人殺死的戰爭 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 我們繼續試著建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從戰爭的第二次世界大戰結束後 , 我們走進冷戰 , 加入寒冷的戰爭 , 然後我們進入冷戰 , 聖戰 , 最後我們進入冷戰 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的目標是 , 我們不需要建造橋樑 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲的橋樑 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是來自華盛頓特區的一部分 , 北京的大樓 , 和巴勒斯坦的大樓 , 和巴勒斯坦 , 和巴勒斯坦 , 談到如何 , 在這個議題上 , 很大的建築牆壁的一部分 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 幾十年來 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始開始看到這些社區 , 開始看到這些社區 , 開始看到這些社區 , 開始看到這些社群 , 開始看到這些社區開始 , 開始看到這些社區 , 開始看到這些社區開始 ,
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我會說 , 首先 , 開放資源安全是聯合國際網路、社交網絡、私人的溝通 , 並且在社交網路上 , 開放資源安全 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談一下為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為全球公共的共同點都被建造牆壁的威脅 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	我是很明顯的 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 橫跨印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片是怎麼回事 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它有卡蒂娜•路線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	要避免盜獵者 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	piracy是一個非常活躍的威脅 , 在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	piracy也非常活躍在馬拉卡 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	它是活躍的 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海中看到它 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	這是全球運輸系統的百分之十 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時代 , 有20個船員 , 500位馬丁斯特人 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是全球常見的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要思考如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉移到不同的海域 , 網路海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	那時 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們採取了一套信卡詐欺 , 給他們超過10億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟的一部分 。
two trillion a year .	每年有兩兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是在英國的gdp中 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這個網路海 , 我們所知道的 , 基本的基礎是從根本的基礎的基礎 , 卻是很大的基礎 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	另一件我擔心的事情是威脅 , 來自阿富汗 , 來自阿富汗 , 來自阿富汗 , 來自阿富汗 , 到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心古柯鹼來自西北部 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心人們販賣的非法武器和販賣 , 或許我們擔心人類販賣 , 可能 , 我們擔心的是非法武器和販賣的成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	交易運行在海中 , 但在全球各地的另一部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴各位 , 這是一張非常高科技的美國海軍軍隊 , 希望我能告訴各位 , 這是一張非常高科技的美國海軍軍隊 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 它是用藥品用藥品的裝置 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它在南美洲的叢林中建造 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們拿了六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	第四個 , 複雜的溝通 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在人類、武器、武器中 , 被威脅到全球共通的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	咱們來看看阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的一場 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	8%到90%的美國人 , 來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到 , 當然恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是阿拉達亞的舞台 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的急迫性 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以這種恐怖主義的全球共通點是全球共通的一部分 , 我們必須解決 。
so here we are , 21st century .	這是21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道20世紀的工具無法工作 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我會說 , 我們不會把安全帶到槍枝的安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會把安全帶到槍枝的安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要使用軍隊力量的力量 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們必須做得很好 , 和競爭 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 公共和網路的聯繫 , 開放的資源安全是關於國際、互聯網、社交網路的聯繫 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我給各位幾個例子 , 說明這如何運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 這些是阿富汗軍人 。
they are all holding books .	他們都是有書籍的 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 , 我以為我閱讀了這位年輕男性和女性 , 在2030年代的年輕男性和女性 , 很高興 。 」
you would be correct .	你會正確 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	85%無法讀到阿富汗的安全力量 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班的教育在日期中 , 這些男人和女人都學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在書裡 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們正在教導他們閱讀文法 , 透過奈及和私人企業合作 , 與私人企業合作 , 與私人合作夥伴合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教導了超過200 , 000個阿富汗安全力 , 來閱讀和寫作 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你閱讀和寫在阿富汗時 , 你通常會把鉛筆放在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	當這些年輕男性和女性畢業時 , 他們把錢放在口袋裡 , 把錢放在口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這裡有五十個國家 , 參與這個任務 , 包括這些發展機構和私人的公共和私人 , 這些發展機構和私人合作 , 將國際聯繫起來 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	現在 , 我們也教他們 , 當然 , 但是我會說 , 開放資源安全效應 , 當然 , 我會說 , 開放資源安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰士 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做 「 舒適 」 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一個西方的船 , 叫做 「 西方 」 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這樣一來 , 在加勒比海和東南美洲的海岸中 , 營養了病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的情況下 , 他們會做四十萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不是被軍隊的組合 , 而是由軍人主義組織的結合 , 由軍隊的結合 , 為人道組織:合作 , 希望 , 專案 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織有志工 。
interagency physicians come out .	醫師們出來了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這樣 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的母親兩天來到眼睛診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被關閉時 , 他突然看著 , 說: 「 mamamama , mundoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	通過四十萬個病人治療 , 這種公共和安全的力量 , 你開始看到創造安全力量的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到籃球玩家 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能否選出兩位美國軍士兵在照片裡 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是兩個年輕男孩的一部分 。 這是一系列的美國和加勒比海 , 美國和加勒比海 , 美國和加勒比海 , 美國和加勒比海 , 美國和加勒比海 , 全部都在美國和加勒比海 , 美國和加勒比海 , 全部都在美國和加勒比海中 , 美國和加勒比海 , 都在南美洲和加勒比海 , 在那裡 , 全部都在美國和加勒比海中 , 美國和加勒比海 , 在那裡 , 全部都在美國和加勒比海 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它顯示了男性和女性的關係 , 關於女性的關係 , 以及我所說的角色 , 能夠為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	另外一個觀點就是在災難的角度上 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機在2004年被殺死了250 , 000人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在所有這些情況下 , 大約三十萬人死亡 , 大約三十萬人死亡 , 在巴基斯坦的北部 , 在巴基斯坦的2005年 , 一百五千人死亡 , 在巴基斯坦的國際活動中 , 海地基地震 , 海地地震 , 在巴基斯坦 , 在巴基斯坦 , 2005年 , 在巴基斯坦 , 兩萬五千人死亡 , 在巴基斯坦 , 海地基金會 , 在巴基斯坦 , 在巴基斯坦 , 在巴基斯坦 , 在巴基斯坦 , 兩萬五千人死亡 。

i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我會給你們另一個例子 , 這是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦的一場演講中 , 跟你們說 , 我在倫敦的一場演講中 , 我說 , 我跟你們說 , 我是臉書 , 朋友我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽起來有點笑 。

and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是 , 早上 , 我有幾百名臉書朋友 , 來自印尼和芬蘭 , 說: 「 我們聽你需要一個朋友 , 說: 「 我們聽過你需要朋友 , 說: 「 我們聽過你需要一個朋友 , 不然 , 誰會說: 「 艾米德 , 我們聽你需要朋友 , 什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何傳遞訊息 , 而這些社群網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我先舉個手指 。

i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他提醒我們 , 我不會希望任何人離開房間 , 我們不需要有能力、競爭者 , 才能創造出真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們所做的 , 我們所做的 , 我們要保護自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由、自由言論 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命並不是一股流行 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要一軍軍隊 , 不必要有軍隊 , 不需要軍隊 , 不必是軍隊 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會說 , 生命是一場混亂 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須在這個21世紀的安全中 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀的安全、國際、互相溝通、國際、互相溝通、國際、互相溝通的力量 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	今天我要談維基百科 , 我用維基百科 , 維基百科 , 維基百科 , 不用維基百科 , 維基百科都不用維基百科 , 透過維基百科 , 維基百科 , 維基百科都不用維基百科 , 維基百科都不用維基百科 , 維基百科 , 維基百科都沒有用維基百科 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每一天 , 每一天 , 有數千人收入資訊 , 每一天 , 有數千人參與資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 不是我們所有人都想在一起的 。
